## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x001A [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x001E)
  1: 0x001D [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_001E:
  2: 0x001E [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Lock player control
  3: 0x0020 [0x1E] EventEntity looks at LocalPlayer and starts talking
  4: 0x0025 [0x6F] WAIT_FRAME_DELAY: Yield until WaitTime reaches zero
  5: 0x0026 [0x70] WAIT_ENTITY_RENDER_FLAG: Wait while EventEntity->Render.Flags3 bit 2 is set (cancel turn if not)
  6: 0x0027 [0x41] GET_BIT_WORK_RANGE(start_bit=0*, end_bit=3*, source=Work_Zone[2], result=ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0])
```
